  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Account</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

[Node](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Node)

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

Type Fields

id:[ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

`Account` Id.

users**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

): [UserItems](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/UserItems)

List and search `UserItems`.

userGroups**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

): [UserGroupItems](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/UserGroupItems)

List and search `UserGroupItems`.

search**(**

Beta

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

query: [AccountQueryInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AccountQueryInput)

): [AccountSearchItems](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AccountSearchItems)

<page>
  <title>Query: asset</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/queries/asset</url>
  <content>Query Field

Retrieve `Asset` details by Id.

Fields of Asset

The `creator` is the `User` who created the asset on Frontify.

DateTime of the `Asset` creation.

The `modifier` is the `User` who last modified the asset on Frontify.

DateTime of the `Asset`'s last modification.

Description of the `Asset`.

List of `Asset`'s `Attachments`.

External Id of the `Asset`.

**BETA** `Asset` will be available only during the defined `DateTime` range.When `null` it represents an unspecified start and/or open-ended date.

`Asset` available until date.

List of `Asset`'s licenses.

Metadata values details. This field will be removed. Use `customMetadata` instead.

Represents the conversion status of the `Asset`. Example: FINISHED.

relatedAssets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `Asset` items related to `Asset`.

comments**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `AssetComment` items for `Asset`.

`Asset` permissions of the current `User`.

List of `CustomMetadataProperty` items and values associated to `Asset`.

**BETA** The `WorkflowTask` this `Asset` is linked to.

**BETA** Background color of the `Asset` preview.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Interface: Asset</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Asset</url>
  <content>Interface

`AssetInterface` for `Asset` returnable types.

Implemented by

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.Following types all implement this interface and must have all fields of this interface present.The `__typename` field resolves to a String which lets you differentiate different data types from each other on the client.

Type Fields

The `creator` is the `User` who created the asset on Frontify.

DateTime of the `Asset` creation.

The `modifier` is the `User` who last modified the asset on Frontify.

DateTime of the `Asset`'s last modification.

Description of the `Asset`.

List of `Asset`'s `Attachments`.

External Id of the `Asset`.

**BETA** `Asset` will be available only during the defined `DateTime` range.When `null` it represents an unspecified start and/or open-ended date.

`Asset` available until date.

List of `Asset`'s licenses.

Metadata values details. This field will be removed. Use `customMetadata` instead.

Represents the conversion status of the `Asset`. Example: FINISHED.

relatedAssets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `Asset` items related to `Asset`.

comments**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `AssetComment` items for `Asset`.

`Asset` permissions of the current `User`.

List of `CustomMetadataProperty` items and values associated to `Asset`.

**BETA** The `WorkflowTask` this `Asset` is linked to.

**BETA** Background color of the `Asset` preview.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Query: brands</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/queries/brands</url>
  <content>Query Field

Retrieve `Brand` list for current `Account`.

Fields of Brand

color:[String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

Deprecated, Removal: 2023-01-01

`Brand` color. This field will be removed. Use `rgbaColor` instead.

projects**(**

Deprecated, Removal: 2023-01-01

Retrieve all `Projects`. This field will be removed. Use `libraries` or `workspaceProjects` instead.

**BETA** Search for the assets on the brand level.

libraries**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Retrieve all `Library` items.

workspaceProjects**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Retrieve all `Workspace` items.

`Brand` `CustomMetadataProperty` items list.

**BETA** Retrieve all `CreativeTemplate` items.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Interface: Library</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Library</url>
  <content>Interface

`LibraryInterface` for `Library` returnable types.

Implemented by

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.Following types all implement this interface and must have all fields of this interface present.The `__typename` field resolves to a String which lets you differentiate different data types from each other on the client.

Type Fields

assetCount:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)

Deprecated, Removal: 2024-07-01

Amount of `Assets` contained in this `Library`. This field will be removed. Use `assets`.`total` instead.

Retrieve list of all `MetadataFields` belonging to this `Library`. This field will be removed. Use `customMetadataProperties` instead.

assets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Search or list `Assets` in this `Library`.

Retrieve list of all `Licenses` belonging to this `Library`.

collections**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

List `Collection` type items within a `Library`.

Browse the `Library`'s `SubFolderItems` and `AssetItems`.

Check current `User` permissions in a specific `Library`.

**BETA** The `Workflow` belonging to the given `Library`.

List of `CustomMetadataProperty` items belonging to a `Library`.</content>
</page>

  <title>Query: creativeTemplate</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/queries/creativeTemplate</url>
  <content>Query Field

creativeTemplate(id: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!):[CreativeTemplate](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/CreativeTemplate)

Beta


--------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

**BETA** Retrieve a `CreativeTemplate` item by Id.

Arguments

id: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

Beta

**BETA** `CreativeTemplate` Id.

Fields of CreativeTemplate

id:[ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

Beta

**BETA** `CreativeTemplate` id.

brandId:[ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

Beta

**BETA** Id of the `Brand` of the `CreativeTemplate`.

name:[String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)!

Beta

**BETA** Name of the `CreativeTemplate`.

description:[String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

Beta

**BETA** Description of the `CreativeTemplate`.

pages:\[[CreativeTemplatePage](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/CreativeTemplatePage)!\]!

Beta

**BETA** Retrieve list of all `CreativeTemplatePage` items belonging to `CreativeTemplate`.

variables:\[[CreativeTemplateVariable](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/CreativeTemplateVariable)!\]!

Beta

**BETA** Retrieve list of all `CreativeTemplateVariable` items belonging to `CreativeTemplate`.</content>
</page>

  <content>Query Field

project(id: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!):[Project](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Project)

  <title>Mutation: uninstallWebhook</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/mutations/uninstallWebhook</url>
  <content>Mutation

uninstallWebhook():[UninstallWebhook](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/UninstallWebhook)
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------------

Uninstall `Webhook`. Requires `basic:write` and `webhook:write` scopes to be accessible and `Project` permission level `EDIT`.

**All mutations** have exactly **one** input field called `input` with a **unique input and return type**. This is useful to write mutations with variables, so there is always one single variable per mutation. This makes it easier to use and reuse them.

Input fields of UninstallWebhookInput

Id of the `Webhook` to be uninstalled.

Fields of UninstallWebhook</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Mutation: uploadFile</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/mutations/uploadFile</url>
  <content>Mutation

Upload a new file. This stores the binary file temporarily so it can be then permanently linked to a specific type (ie. `Asset`, `Attachment`, `Revision`) after the upload is complete by using a different mutation. Requires `basic:write` scope to be accessible.

**All mutations** have exactly **one** input field called `input` with a **unique input and return type**. This is useful to write mutations with variables, so there is always one single variable per mutation. This makes it easier to use and reuse them.

Input fields of UploadFileInput

`File` name. This value will be passed on to the `fileId` input variable used in file mutations such as `createAsset`, `replaceAsset`, `createAttachment` or `addAssetPreviewImage`.

`File` chunk size in bytes. Value must be integer between 5MB and 1GB.

Fields of UploadFile

Arrays with upload `Urls` to upload the file.</content>
</page>

Type Fields

total:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Total amount of results.

page:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Current page number.

limit:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Number of results per page.

hasNextPage:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Indicates if a next page is available or not

items:\[[AccountSearchResult](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AccountSearchResult)\]

List of `AccountSearchResult` items.</content>

  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

[Node](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Node)

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

[User](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/User)

`UserInterface` for `User` returnable types.

Type Fields

id:[ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

`AccountUser` Id.

email:[Email](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Email)!

`AccountUser` email.

name:[String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

`AccountUser` name.

avatar:[Url](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Url)

`AccountUser` avatar.</content>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: AssetAttachment</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetAttachment</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

`AttachmentInterface` for `Attachment` returnable types.

Type Fields

The `creator` is the `User` who created this `Attachment`.

`DateTime` of the `Attachment` creation.

The `modifier` is the `User` who last modified this `Attachment`.

`DateTime` of the `Attachment`last modification.

Filename of the `Attachment` `File`.

Mediatype (MIME) of the `Attachment`.

External Id of the `Attachment`.

Extension of the `Attachment` `File`.

Size of the `Attachment` `File` in bytes.

downloadUrl**(**

validityInDays: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)

Signed `Url` to download the original `AssetAttachment` from Frontify.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: AssetComment</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetComment</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

`CommentInterface` for `Comment` returnable types.

Type Fields

`User` who created the `AssetComment`.

`DateTime` of the `AssetComment`'s creation.

`User` who last modified the `AssetComment`.

`DateTime` of the `AssetComment`'s last modification.

The content of the `AssetComment`. Contains `User` mentions in the format `@[user:USER_ID].`

Mentioned `User` list in the `content` field.

Indicates if an `AssetComment` is resolved or not.

replies**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

`AssetComment`'s `AssetCommentReplyItems` list.

The `AssetComment` `Marking` if it exists.

`AssetComment` permissions of the current `User`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: AssetCommentReply</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetCommentReply</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

`CommentInterface` for `Comment` returnable types.

Type Fields

The id of the current `AssetCommentReply`.

The `User` representing the creator.

The `DateTime` of creation.

The `User` representing the last modifier.

The `DateTime` of the last modification.

The content of the `AssetCommentReply`. Contains `User` mentions in the format `@[user:USER_ID].`

Mentioned `User` list in the `content` field.</content>
</page>

  <title>Object Type: AssetLocation</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetLocation</url>
  <content>brand:[AssetLocationBrand](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetLocationBrand)

`Brand` location of the `Asset`.

library:[AssetLocationLibrary](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetLocationLibrary)

`Library` location of the `Asset`.

workspaceProject:[AssetLocationWorkspaceProject](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetLocationWorkspaceProject)

`WorkspaceProject` location of the `Asset`.

folder:[AssetLocationFolder](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetLocationFolder)

`Folder` location of the `Asset`.</content>
</page>

  <content>Object Type

No description

Type Fields

A list of `Breadcrumb` items representing the parent folders structure for the current `Folder`.</content>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: AssetUserPermissions</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetUserPermissions</url>
  <content>canEdit:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Check if current user has `Asset` editing permissions for a specific `Asset`.

canDelete:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Check if current user has `Asset` deleting permissions for a specific `Asset`.

canDownload:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Check if current user has `Asset` download permissions for a specific `Asset`.

canComment:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Check if current user has `Comment` creation permissions for a specific `Asset`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: Audio</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Audio</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

`AssetInterface` for `Asset` returnable types.

Type Fields

The `User` who created the `Asset`.

`DateTime` of the `Asset` creation.

The `User` who last modified the `Asset`.

`DateTime` of the `Asset` last modification.

Description of the `Asset`.

`Attachment` items linked to `Asset`.

External Id of the `Asset`.

List of `Tag` items linked to `Asset`

`MetadataValue` items linked to `Asset`. This field will be removed. Use `customMetadata` instead.

`ExternalProduct` items linked to `Asset`. This field will be removed.

**BETA** `Asset` will be available only during the defined `DateTime` range.When `null` it represents an unspecified start and/or open-ended date.

`Asset` available until date.

`License` items linked to `Asset`.

Represents the Author of the `Asset`. Example: Photographer Name.

Represents the conversion status of the `Asset`. Example: FINISHED.

relatedAssets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `Asset` items related to `Asset`.

comments**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `AssetComment` items for `Asset`.

Current `User` `Asset` permissions.

List of `CustomMetadataProperty` items and values associated to `Asset`.

**BETA** The `WorkflowTask` this `Asset` is linked to.

**BETA** Background color of the `Asset` preview.

Original filename of the `Asset` `File`.

Size of the `Asset` `File` in bytes.

Extension of the `Asset` `File`.

downloadUrl**(**

validityInDays: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)

Signed `Url` to download the original `Audio` type file.

Preview `Url` of converted `Audio` file in mp3 format.

Provides a `Url` for the custom user defined thumbnail or a system generated one when possible.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: BrandSearchItems</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/BrandSearchItems</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

This is a paginated list, containing items of type `BrandSearchResult`. You can find more information about how pagination works in our Developer Portal under Pagination. **Edges** have additional metadata related to the `BrandSearchResult` available.

Type Fields

Number of results per page.

Indicates if a next page is available or not

List of `BrandSearchResult` items.

List of `BrandSearchResult` edges.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: Collection</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Collection</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

[Node](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Node)

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

Type Fields

id:[ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

`Collection` Id.

name:[String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)!

`Collection` name.

assets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

): [AssetItems](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetItems)!

`Collection`'s `Asset` items list.

isPrivate:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)

Deprecated

**DEPRECATED** `Collection`'s privacy state setting. This field will be removed. | Date: 2024-01-01T00:00:00.000+00:00

currentUserPermissions:[CollectionUserPermissions](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/CollectionUserPermissions)!

`Collection`'s permissions of the current `User`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: CollectionItems</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/CollectionItems</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

This is a paginated list, containing items of type `Collection`. You can find more information about how pagination works in our Developer Portal under Pagination.

Type Fields

total:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Total amount of results.

page:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Current page number.

limit:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Number of results per page.

hasNextPage:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Indicates if a next page is available or not

items:\[[Collection](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Collection)\]

List of `Collection` items.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: CollectionUserPermissions</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/CollectionUserPermissions</url>
  <content>canAddAssets:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Check if the current user can add `Assets` in this `Collection`.

canRemoveAssets:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Check if the current user can remove `Assets` from this `Collection`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: Document</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Document</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

`AssetInterface` for `Asset` returnable types.

Type Fields

The `User` who created the `Asset`.

`DateTime` of the `Asset` creation.

The `User` who last modified the `Asset`.

`DateTime` of the `Asset` last modification.

Description of the `Asset`.

`Attachment` items linked to `Asset`.

External Id of the `Asset`.

List of `Tag` items linked to `Asset`

`MetadataValue` items linked to `Asset`. This field will be removed. Use `customMetadata` instead.

`ExternalProduct` items linked to `Asset`. This field will be removed.

**BETA** `Asset` will be available only during the defined `DateTime` range.When `null` it represents an unspecified start and/or open-ended date.

`Asset` available until date.

`License` items linked to `Asset`.

Represents the Author of the `Asset`. Example: Photographer Name.

Represents the conversion status of the `Asset`. Example: FINISHED.

relatedAssets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `Asset` items related to `Asset`.

comments**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Paginated list of `AssetComment` items for `Asset`.

Current `User` `Asset` permissions.

List of `CustomMetadataProperty` items and values associated to `Asset`.

**BETA** The `WorkflowTask` this `Asset` is linked to.

**BETA** Background color of the `Asset` preview.

Original filename of the `Asset` `File`.

Size of the `Asset` `File` in bytes.

Extension of the `Asset` `File`.

Preview `Url` which has optional `width`, `height` and `page` arguments. If parameters are not specified, a `Url` without any parameters will be returned.

Provides a `Url` for the custom user defined thumbnail or a system generated one when possible.

downloadUrl**(**

validityInDays: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)

Signed `Url` to download the original `Document` type file.

`Document` focal point position. Example: `[0.4803, 0.4340]`.

`Document` width in pixels.

`Document` height in pixels.

`Document` total number of pages.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: DocumentLibrary</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/DocumentLibrary</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

`LibraryInterface` for `Library` returnable types.

Type Fields

**DEPRECATED** Amount of `Assets` contained in the `Library`/`Workspace`. This field will be removed. Use `assets`.`total` instead. | Date: 2024-07-01T00:00:00.000+00:00

assets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

Search or list `Assets` in the `Library`/`Workspace`.

`Library`/`Workspace` `License` items list.

**DEPRECATED** `Library`/`Workspace` `MetadataField` items list. This field will be removed. Use `customMetadataProperties` instead. | Date: 2025-01-01T00:00:00.000+00:00

**BETA** The `Workflow` belonging to the given `Library`/`Workspace`.

Browse the `Library` `SubFolderItems` and `AssetItems`.

`Library` permissions of the current `User`.

Retrieve list of all `CustomMetadataProperty` items belonging to `Library`.

collections**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

`Library` `Collection` items list.</content>

  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

[Node](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Node)

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

[Webhook](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Webhook)

`WebhookInterface` for `Webhook` returnable types.

Type Fields

id:[ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

`Webhook` Id.

The `creator` is the `User` who created the `Webhook`.

createdAt:[DateTime](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/DateTime)!

DateTime of the `Webhook` creation.

name:[String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)!

`Webhook` name.

secret:[String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)!

The randomly generated secret of the current `Webhook`.

notificationUrl:[Url](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Url)!

The `Url` which will be called by the `Webhook`

project:[Project](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Project)!

<page>
  <title>Object Type: SimpleMarking</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/SimpleMarking</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

[Marking](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Marking)

Interface representing a visual `Marking` (highlighted point/area) of an `Asset`.

Type Fields

position:[MarkingPosition](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingPosition)!

The `Marking` position in percent relative to the top left corner of the `Asset`.

dimensions:[MarkingDimensions](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingDimensions)

The `Marking` dimensions in percent of `Asset` dimensions.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: SubFolder</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/SubFolder</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Implemented Interfaces

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

`FolderInterface` for `Folder` returnable types.

Type Fields

The `User` who created the `SubFolder`.

`DateTime` of the `SubFolder` creation.

The `User` who last modified the `SubFolder`.

`DateTime` of the last `SubFolder` modification.

A list of `Breadcrumb` items representing the parent folders structure for the current `SubFolder`.

subFolders**(**

Deprecated, Removal: 2024-07-01

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

The `SubFolderItems` of the current `SubFolder`. This field will be removed. Use `folders` instead.

folders**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

The `FolderItems` of the current `Folder`.

assets**(**

limit: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 25

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int) **=** 1

The `AssetItems` in the current `SubFolder`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Object Type: SubFolderItems</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/SubFolderItems</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

This is a paginated list, containing items of type `SubFolder`. You can find more information about how pagination works in our Developer Portal under Pagination.

Type Fields

total:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Total amount of results.

page:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Current page number.

limit:[Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)!

Number of results per page.

hasNextPage:[Boolean](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean)!

Indicates if a next page is available or not

items:\[[SubFolder](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/SubFolder)\]

List of type `SubFolder`</content>
</page>

  <title>Object Type: Tag</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Tag</url>
  <content>Object Type

No description

Type Fields

`Tag` source indicating how the tag was linked to the `Asset`. AUTO: created by AI `Asset` recognition. MANUAL: manually added.</content>

The `User` who created the `Asset`.

External Id of the `Asset`.

List of `Tag` items linked to `Asset`

`ExternalProduct` items linked to `Asset`. This field will be removed.

`Asset` available until date.

`License` items linked to `Asset`.

Represents the Author of the `Asset`. Example: Photographer Name.

Represents the conversion status of the `Asset`. Example: FINISHED.

  <title>Input Object Type: AssetQueryFilterConditionInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetQueryFilterConditionInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

Defines which property of the `Asset` is compared to the provided value.

Defines how the value of the `Asset` is compared to the provided value.

The value which is compared against the property of the `Asset`.

**REQUIRED** for type `METADATA_VALUE` to identify which metadata field it is compared against. You can find all available `metadataFields` on the project.

customMetadataPropertyId: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)

**REQUIRED** for type `CUSTOM_METADATA_VALUE` to identify which `CustomMetadataProperty` it is compared against. You can find all available `CustomMetadataProperty` on the project.</content>
</page>

  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

andConditions: \[[AssetQueryFilterConditionInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetQueryFilterConditionInput)\]

The Asset must pass **all conditions** in this List to be present in the result set.

orConditions: \[[AssetQueryFilterConditionInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetQueryFilterConditionInput)\]

The Asset must pass **at least one condition** in this List to be present in the result set.</content>

  <title>Input Object Type: BrandQueryInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/BrandQueryInput</url>
  <content>term: [String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

Search term used to retrieve matched results.

sortBy: [BrandQuerySortByInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/BrandQuerySortByInput) **=** RELEVANCE

Sort order of matched results.

searchIn: \[[BrandSearchQuerySource](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/BrandSearchQuerySource)\] **=** \[EVERYWHERE\]

Deprecated, Removal: 2023-07-01

Specify the sources of the matched results. This field will be removed. Use `filter.sources` instead.

filter: [BrandQueryFilterInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/BrandQueryFilterInput)

Use filters to reduce the set of matched results.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: AssetQueryInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetQueryInput</url>
  <content>filter: [AssetQueryFilterInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetQueryFilterInput)

Use filters to reduce the set of matched `Asset` items by complex filtering.

inFolder: [AssetQueryInFolderInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetQueryInFolderInput)

Limit the result set to a specific `Folder` of this `Library`.

sortBy: [AssetQueryFilterSortType](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetQueryFilterSortType)

Sort set of the matched `AssetItems`.

externalId: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)

Limit the result set by the externalId of an `Asset`.

search: [String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

Limit the result set by the search term.

type: \[[AssetType](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetType)\]

Deprecated, Removal: 2022-07-01

Filter the `Asset` types present in the result set. This field will be removed. Use `types` instead.

types: \[[AssetType](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/AssetType)\]

Limit the result set by the `Asset` types.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: CreateAssetInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/CreateAssetInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

projectId: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)

Deprecated, Removal: 2023-07-01

`Library` or `Workspace` Id. This value is ignored if `parentId` is set. This field will be removed. Use `parentId` instead.

File Id. Signed Id returned in `uploadFile`.

`Asset` title or display name.

Add `Asset` copyright details.

List of tags to create with `Asset`

Skip file's EXIF metadata. When true, it will ignore all file metadata contents.

An array of strings representing the directory, if a folder does not exist, it is created. Example: \["My Folder", "Sub-Folder"\] will create the necessary folders if they do not yet exist and place the `Asset` in it. **Important:** Cannot be used in conjunction with `parentId` that is from a `Folder`.

The parent Id, where the `Asset` should be located in. Should either be a `Library`, `WorkspaceProject` or `Folder` Id. **Important:** Cannot be used in conjunction with `directory` if the Id is from a `Folder`.

Deprecated, Removal: 2022-07-01

`Asset` workflow status. Workflow logic will be automatically managed if not properly set. This field will be removed.

`Asset` will become available only during the interval.When undefined or `null` the `Asset` will be immediately and indefinitely available.

`Asset` will expire once the defined date is reached.

Represents the Author of the `Asset`. Example: Photographer Name

**BETA** Background color of the `Asset` preview.</content>
</page>

  <content>projectId: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

Id of the `Project` you want to invite `User` to.

email: [Email](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Email)!

Email address of the `User` you would like to invite.

permission: [ProjectPermission](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ProjectPermission)! **=** VIEW

`Project` permission level of the `User` you are inviting.

validFrom: [DateTime](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/DateTime)

Start `Date` for `User` access permission validity.

validTo: [DateTime](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/DateTime)

End `Date` for `User` access permission validity.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: LibraryQueryInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/LibraryQueryInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

**BETA** Sort order of the `Library` query result set.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: MarkingInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingInput</url>
  <content>position: [MarkingPositionInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingPositionInput)

The `Marking` position in percentage, in relation to the top left corner of the `Asset`.

dimensions: [MarkingDimensionsInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingDimensionsInput)

The `Marking` dimensions in percentage of the annotated subject dimensions.

timeframe: [MarkingTimeframeInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingTimeframeInput)

The timeframe of the `Marking` area in percentage of total video length. Applicable to `Video` type `Assets` only.

page: [Int](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int)

The `Marking` page. Applicable to `Assets` with the type `Document` only.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: MarkingDimensionsInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingDimensionsInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

The width of the `Marking` area in percentage of the annotated subject total width.

The height of the `Marking` area in percentage of the annotated subject total height.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: MarkingPositionInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingPositionInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

The horizontal position of the `Marking` in percentage, in relation to the `Asset` top left corner.

The vertical position of the `Marking` in percentage, in relation to the `Asset` top left corner.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: MarkingTimeframeInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MarkingTimeframeInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

The start of the `Marking` area in percentage of total video length. Defaults to video start (0) when the timeframe input property is set.

The end of the `Marking` area in percentage of total video length. Defaults to video end (1) when the timeframe input property is set.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: MoveFoldersInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MoveFoldersInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

Ids of the `Folder` items to be moved.

Id of the destination entity where `Folder` items should be moved to. Allows `Library`/`Workspace`/`Folder` Ids only.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: MoveWorkflowTaskInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MoveWorkflowTaskInput</url>
  <content>Input Object Type

No description

Input Fields

workflowStatusId: [ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!

Beta

**BETA** The Id of the destination `WorkflowStatus`.

workflowTaskIds: \[[ID](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID)!\]!

Beta

**BETA** List of `WorkflowTask` Ids to move. Limited to 100 Ids.

statusEnterMessage: [String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

Beta

**BETA** `WorkflowTask` enter message. Optionally required by a `EnterRule` of the given `WorkflowStatus`.</content>
</page>

No description

Input Fields

<page>
  <title>Input Object Type: UpdateAssetDataInput</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/UpdateAssetDataInput</url>
  <content>title: [String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

`Asset` title or display name.

filename: [String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

`Asset` filename, including extension.

description: [String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

`Asset` description.

copyright: [UpdateCopyrightInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/UpdateCopyrightInput)

Change `Asset` copyright details.

expiresAt: [DateTime](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/DateTime)

Modify expiry date. `Asset` will expire once the defined date is reached.

author: [String](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String)

Represents the Author of the `Asset`. Example: Photographer Name.

previewBackgroundColor: [RgbaColorInput](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/RgbaColorInput)

Beta

**BETA** Background color of the `Asset` preview.</content>
</page>

  <title>Interface: Attachment</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Attachment</url>
  <content>Interface

`AttachmentInterface` for `Attachment` returnable types.

Implemented by

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.Following types all implement this interface and must have all fields of this interface present.The `__typename` field resolves to a String which lets you differentiate different data types from each other on the client.

Type Fields

The `User` who created the `Attachment` on Frontify.

`DateTime` of the `Attachment` creation.

The `User` who last modified the `Attachment` on Frontify.

`DateTime` of the `Attachment`'s last modification.

The `Attachment`'s filename.

The `Attachment`'s name or title.

The `Attachment`'s original file extension.

The `Attachment`'s Media (MIME) type.

The `Attachment`'s size in bytes.

The `Attachment`'s External Id.</content>
</page>

`NodeInterface` is the base for all types.

Implemented by

An Interface is an abstract type that includes a certain set of fields that a type must include to implement the interface.Following types all implement this interface and must have all fields of this interface present.The `__typename` field resolves to a String which lets you differentiate different data types from each other on the client.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Union: Project</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Project</url>
  <content>Implemented by

Union types are very similar to interfaces, but they don't get to specify any common fields between the types. The `__typename` field resolves to a String which lets you differentiate different data types from each other on the client.

[MediaLibrary](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/MediaLibrary)

\--

[IconLibrary](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/IconLibrary)

\--

[LogoLibrary](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/LogoLibrary)

\--

[DocumentLibrary](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/DocumentLibrary)

\--

[Workspace](https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Workspace)

\--</content>
</page>

Enum Values

RELEVANCE

NEWEST

OLDEST

Sorts the results by the oldest `Assets`.

TITLE\_ASCENDING

TITLE\_DESCENDING

sorts the results descending by the title of the `Assets`.</content>

<page>
  <title>Enum: ConditionType</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ConditionType</url>
  <content>Enum

Condition types. A Condition defines which field value of the `Asset` is compared against a given value. We currently support 4 different kinds of Conditions on `Assets`:

*   **TAG**: Refers to a tag of the `Asset`.
*   **METADATA\_VALUE**: Refers to a value of a custom `MetadataField` of an `Asset`.
*   **CUSTOM\_METADATA\_VALUE**: Refers to a value of a `CustomMetadata` of an `Asset`.
*   **EXTERNAL\_ID**: Refers to the `externalId` assigned to the `Asset`.
*   **FILE\_EXTENSION**: Refers to the file extension of an `Asset`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Enum: WorkflowStatusEnterRule</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/WorkflowStatusEnterRule</url>
  <content>Enum

A rule which needs to be satisfied for a `WorkflowTask` to enter a given `WorkflowStatus`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Enum: WorkspaceProjectQuerySort</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/WorkspaceProjectQuerySort</url>
  <content>Enum

Query sorting option. Defines how the search results should be sorted.

Enum Values

NEWEST

Sorts the results by the newest entry.

OLDEST

Sorts the results by the oldest entry\`.

NEWEST\_ACTIVITY

Sorts the results by the newest activity entry.

OLDEST\_ACTIVITY

Sorts the results by the oldest activity entry.</content>
</page>

  <content>Enum

`WorkspaceProject` state filter.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: Any</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Any</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `Any` scalar type represents any of the supported types: Null, Integer, Float, String, Boolean, Enum, Object and List.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: BigInt</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/BigInt</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `BigInt` scalar type represents big integers (2^63 signed).</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: DateTime</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/DateTime</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `DateTime` scalar type represents datetime data in RFC3339\_EXTENDED format (ie. 2001-12-31T22:10:30.000+00:00)</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: Boolean</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Boolean</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `Boolean` scalar type represents `true` or `false`.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: Email</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Email</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `Email` scalar type represents email addresses.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: ID</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/ID</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `ID` scalar type represents a unique identifier, often used to refetch an object or as key for a cache. The ID type appears in a JSON response as a String; however, it is not intended to be human-readable. When expected as an input type, any string (such as `"4"`) or integer (such as `4`) input value will be accepted as an ID.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: Percent</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Percent</url>
  <content>Scalar

Represents an integer or a float value between `0` and `1`, corresponding to percentage values between 0% and 100% (both inclusive).</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: Int</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Int</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `Int` scalar type represents non-fractional signed whole numeric values. Int can represent values between -(2^31) and 2^31 - 1.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: Float</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Float</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `Float` scalar type represents signed double-precision fractional values as specified by [IEEE 754](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/IEEE_floating_point).</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: RgbColorChannel</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/RgbColorChannel</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `RgbColorChannel` scalar represents an integer value between 0 and 255 (both inclusive).</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: Url</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/Url</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `Url` scalar type represents absolute urls.</content>
</page>

<page>
  <title>Scalar: String</title>
  <url>https://frontify.github.io/graphql-reference/type/String</url>
  <content>Scalar

The `String` scalar type represents textual data, represented as UTF-8 character sequences. The String type is most often used by GraphQL to represent free-form human-readable text.</content>
</page>
